2019-08-25 00:11:19.938 +03:00 [INF] Executed DbCommand (5ms) [Parameters=[@__id_0='?' (DbType = Int32)], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT [x.Comments].[Id], [x.Comments].[Content], [x.Comments].[CreateDate], [x.Comments].[bookId], [t].[Id]
FROM [Comments] AS [x.Comments]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT TOP(1) [x0].[Id]
    FROM [Book] AS [x0]
    WHERE [x0].[Id] = @__id_0
    ORDER BY [x0].[Id]
) AS [t] ON [x.Comments].[bookId] = [t].[Id]
